name:W‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçs‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äç‚Äô‚Äçs

info:Stayed in May 2024

posted:Posted June 2, 2024
msg:This trip of three days and two nights was arranged because of my wife‚Äôs wedding anniversary.
Take a break and enjoy the quality of life in a leisurely mood!
So take your time and read it!
First we arrived at the hotel at noon and were ready to store our luggage!
The female staff in charge does not need to speak Cantonese, but she is also very enthusiastic and serves with a smile.
During this period, another employee passed by and took the initiative to help place our luggage.
The staff I met afterwards were all very nice! 
Especially the staff in the lobby restaurant!
The older ones are kind and steady, while the younger ones are enthusiastic, polite and full of energy!
Everyone shows a customer-oriented spirit, which is rare!
As for the shortcomings, the charger in the room does not have type C and is outdated.
The TV broadcast failed to reach the 2K level, especially when watching KBS, it was a bit blurry!
If I were to be picky about the restaurant, I would say the appearance of the intercom!
It is suitable for employees who usually wear denim aprons at work.
But for higher-level employees who wear suits, it affects their appearance, and the back of the coat is bulging unsightly!
Their equipment should be replaced to make them more comfortable and increase their sense of belonging!
In summary, this review is positive. Because I received good service, I hope the hotel will improve!
Honestly, the professional service of the staff and the atmosphere displayed by the hotel! For me, I can already give it a high score!
Other hardware is really not a problem! The view from the hotel is also very good!

There was also salmon (it looked like smoked salmon) in the lounge, and a large plate was served. This was not available in the buffet restaurant downstairs (but can Hong Kong-style milk tea also be provided in the lounge?)
There was also a small episode here. When we booked, breakfast was included, but when we went to the buffet restaurant in the morning, the front desk said that the result of the query showed that our reservation did not include breakfast. After it was resolved, it was shown that we had consumed in the restaurant when we checked out.
